I was referred to this office by Cigna HMO for an emergency appointment (tooth ache). At first it was really good; the DA was nice, the dentist listened, and the office was fairly clean.

However, when it came to do any work the office manager was extremely condescending and even cruelly laughed at me when I begged to have my tooth extracted. The prices did not reflect my fee schedule and they added ridiculous additional services like a gingivectomy around the #2 tooth for the nominal fee of $700 out of pocket. A gingivectomy is a cosmetic procedure; there is a procedure for crown lengthening and that IS covered by insurance but dentists are paid less by the insurance and no copay for me. They were willing to unnecessarily cut my gums up so they could squeeze a few more bucks out of me.

I arrived at 10:30am and didn't leave until about 1pm, all they did was take a bunch of x-rays and refused to treat me since I didn't have thousands of dollars to spend in cosmetic procedures on my back teeth. They told me if I wanted the tooth extracted so bad that I could go to a clinic, despite me having insurance. FYI, this office claims they are not accepting ANY HMO business after this month.

They seem to sub out all of their endo and extraction work to specialists, which is common practice because they make less than they would with cosmetic dentistry. Even though they accepted my emergency appointment they told me they could do nothing to treat me until next week. I'm in so much pain and I told them I felt like I might pass out but the office manager just asked me to leave. This office has no respect for their customer's safety or well being. Hoping to find a good dentist before this infected tooth literally kills me, but for now since this office wasted my entire day I will be drinking and crying myself to sleep.</review>

<name>Jen Doyle</name><Date>1523511008960< /Date><rate>5<//rate>< Text>
Formerly Michels' Family Dentistry, recently under new ownership and renamed La Mesa Hills Dentistry, this dentistry does not disappoint.

I've been coming here for almost a year now for myself and my family. We love Dr Fjeldsted's conservative approach. Unlike other dentists, there has been no pressure to do unnecessary treatments.

His staff are friendly and the office is neat and tidy (recently redecorated, very welcoming). The patient's comfort and care is always taken into account.

The office is located in a remodeled house, nestled in the heart of La Mesa. There is street parking available, as well as a small parking lot behind the office. The entrance to the parking lot is located on the west side of the building. Take caution as the driveway is narrow and will not accommodate two vehicles. The office is located next to the La Mesa Historical Society--if heading west and you see the 1900s historical home, you've gone too far and missed the dentistry.

Patient bathroom available.</Text>

They will lock you out of the keypad at the gate, as well as put their own lock on your unit so you can't get in, if you're there for more than 30 minutes, or break one of their other "rules".  I think this is ridiculous, what about people with small cars who can't pack a giant box because it won't fit in the car & need to take all their things, then put the box together, put their items in the box, and then put the box into the unit on-site?  What if you aren't sure where you packed something, go there to retrieve it from the space you pay good money for, and you take too long looking for it?  Here's the answer: You get locked out of the keypad, and your unit double-locked with their company cylinder lock, and they don't even notify you.  So you don't find out that you were "bad" until you try to get in and are denied access at the gate.  There are other ridiculous rules that they will put you in "time-out" for.  When you're sitting at the gate with people behind you trying to get in getting mad at you, everyone behind you has to back up so you can pull out of line, you call them (because they don't call you and let you know that you broke one of their rules & you've been locked out...) and they tell you what you did to be a "bad boy/girl" and inform you that you are in "time out" until up to 5PM the FOLLOWING DAY even if you are calling them during business hours.  I own a business that has no brick-and-mortar location, and if a storage space wasn't vital to my business, I would have taken my property out of there a long time ago.  Unfortunately, I own things that aren't small and cant fit into my house nor sit outside in the elements.  If you don't want to be put in time out like a child, look around the area for another storage space not owned by Rainbow.  By the way, they're not cheap either.  The only reason we rented with them is because they have a 24 hour kiosk a few miles away at the main office, and we were in need of a storage space on Christmas Day.  If we knew what we were getting into with a company that treated their customers this way, to not only do it, but not even bother notifying you, that they're locking you out for exceeding their (un-announced & not even in the contract) 30 minute time limit, we would never have done business with them.  I basically feel like they're treating me as if they think I'm trying to live in or running a meth-lab out of the storage space, when it couldn't be further than the truth... the unit is full of stuffed animals and arcade claw machine games.  Will be moving to another storage unit with a company that treats their customers professionally and as fellow adults as soon as we can.
